                        "import os\nimport time\nimport json\nimport tempfile\nimport requests\nimport threading\nfrom typing import List, Dict\nfrom flask import Flask, render_template_string, request, redirect, url_for, flash\nfrom google.oauth2 import service_account\nfrom googleapiclient.discovery import build\nfrom googleapiclient.http import MediaFileUpload\nfrom openai import OpenAI\nimport smtplib\nfrom email.mime.multipart import MIMEMultipart\nfrom email.mime.application import MIMEApplication\nfrom email.mime.text import MIMEText\n\n# ==================== CONFIGURATION ====================\n\n# MachForm API endpoints and keys (example)\nMACHFORM_FORMS = [\n    {'id': 1, 'api_url': 'https://yourdomain.com/machform/api.php', 'api_key': 'API_KEY_1'},\n    {'id': 2, 'api_url': 'https://yourdomain.com/machform/api.php', 'api_key': 'API_KEY_2'},\n    {'id': 3, 'api_url': 'https://yourdomain.com/machform/api.php', 'api_key': 'API_KEY_3'},\n]\n\n# Google Service Account Credentials JSON file\nGOOGLE_CREDENTIALS_FILE = 'google_service_account.json'\n\n# Google Sheets and Docs IDs\nGOOGLE_SHEET_ID = 'YOUR_GOOGLE_SHEET_ID'\nGOOGLE_DOC_TEMPLATE_ID = 'YOUR_GOOGLE_DOC_TEMPLATE_ID'\nGOOGLE_DRIVE_FOLDER_ID = 'YOUR_GOOGLE_DRIVE_FOLDER_ID'  # For storing PDFs\n\n# OpenAI API Key\nOPENAI_API_KEY = 'sk-...'\n\n# Email settings\nSMTP_SERVER = 'smtp.gmail.com'\nSMTP_PORT = 587\nEMAIL_USER = 'your@email.com'\nEMAIL_PASS = 'your_email_password'\n\n# Salesforce settings\nSALESFORCE_INSTANCE_URL = 'https://your_instance.salesforce.com'\nSALESFORCE_ACCESS_TOKEN = 'YOUR_SF_ACCESS_TOKEN'\nSALESFORCE_OBJECT = 'Student_Report__c'\n\n# Flask secret key\nFLASK_SECRET_KEY = 'supersecretkey'\n\n# =============== MACHFORM DATA EXTRACTION ===============\n\ndef fetch_machform_entries(form):\n    \"\"\"Fetch latest entries from a MachForm form.\"\"\"\n    params = {\n        'api_key': form['api_key'],\n        'form_id': form['id'],\n        'function': 'get_entries',\n        'parameters[is_completed]': 1,\n        'parameters[sort_by]': 'date_created',\n        'parameters[sort_order]': 'desc'\n    }\n    response = requests.get(form['api_url'], params=params)\n    response.raise_for_status()\n    data = response.json()\n    return data.get('entries', [])\n\ndef compile_master_record(entries_list: List[List[Dict]]) -> List[Dict]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Merge entries from all forms based on a common identifier (e.g., email).\n    Returns a list of master records.\n    \"\"\"\n    master = {}\n    for entries in entries_list:\n        for entry in entries:\n            email = entry.get('element_3')  # Assume 'element_3' is email\n            if not email:\n                continue\n            if email not in master:\n                master[email] = {}\n            master[email].update(entry)\n    return list(master.values())\n\n# =============== GOOGLE SHEETS INTEGRATION ===============\n\ndef get_google_services():\n    \"\"\"Authenticate and return Google Sheets, Docs, and Drive services.\"\"\"\n    creds = service_account.Credentials.from_service_account_file(\n        GOOGLE_CREDENTIALS_FILE,\n        scopes=[\n            'https://www.googleapis.com/auth/spreadsheets',\n            'https://www.googleapis.com/auth/drive',\n            'https://www.googleapis.com/auth/documents'\n        ]\n    )\n    sheets_service = build('sheets', 'v4', credentials=creds)\n    docs_service = build('docs', 'v1', credentials=creds)\n    drive_service = build('drive', 'v3', credentials=creds)\n    return sheets_service, docs_service, drive_service\n\ndef append_to_google_sheet(sheets_service, records: List[Dict]):\n    \"\"\"Append records to Google Sheet.\"\"\"\n    values = []\n    for rec in records:\n        values.append([rec.get('element_3', ''), rec.get('element_1', ''), rec.get('element_2', '')])  # Replace placeholders\n    requests_body = [\n        {\n            'replaceAllText': {\n                'containsText': {'text': '{{NAME}}', 'matchCase': True},\n                'replaceText': record.get('element_1', 'N/A')\n            }\n        },\n        {\n            'replaceAllText': {\n                'containsText': {'text': '{{EMAIL}}', 'matchCase': True},\n                'replaceText': record.get('element_3', 'N/A')\n            }\n        },\n        {\n            'replaceAllText': {\n                'containsText': {'text': '{{PATHWAY}}', 'matchCase': True},\n                'replaceText': pathway\n            }\n        }\n        # Add more replacements as needed\n    ]\n    docs_service.documents().batchUpdate(\n        documentId=doc_id,\n        body={'requests': requests_body}\n    ).execute()\n    return doc_id\n\ndef export_doc_to_pdf(drive_service, doc_id: str) -> bytes:\n    \"\"\"Export the Google Doc as PDF and return the bytes.\"\"\"\n    pdf = drive_service.files().export(fileId=doc_id, mimeType='application/pdf').execute()\n    return pdf\n\n# =============== EMAIL SENDING ===============\n\ndef send_email_with_pdf(to_email: str, student_name: str, pdf_bytes: bytes):\n    \"\"\"Send the PDF to the student via email.\"\"\"\n    msg = MIMEMultipart()\n    msg['From'] = EMAIL_USER\n    msg['To'] = to_email\n    msg['Subject'] = f\"Your Personalized Academic Pathway\"\n\n    body = f\"Dear {student_name},\\n\\nPlease find attached your personalized academic pathway.\\n\\nBest regards,\\nAdmissions Team\"\n    msg.attach(MIMEText(body, 'plain'))\n\n    attachment = MIMEApplication(pdf_bytes, _subtype=\"pdf\")\n    attachment.add_header('Content-Disposition', 'attachment', filename=\"Academic_Pathway.pdf\")\n    msg.attach(attachment)\n\n    with smtplib.SMTP(SMTP_SERVER, SMTP_PORT) as server:\n        server.starttls()\n        server.login(EMAIL_USER, EMAIL_PASS)\n        server.sendmail(EMAIL_USER, to_email, msg.as_string())\n\n# =============== SALESFORCE INTEGRATION ===============\n\ndef store_in_salesforce(record: Dict, pdf_bytes: bytes):\n    \"\"\"Store the PDF and metadata in Salesforce.\"\"\"\n    headers = {\n        'Authorization': f'Bearer {SALESFORCE_ACCESS_TOKEN}',\n        'Content-Type': 'application/json'\n    }\n    # Upload PDF as ContentVersion\n    files = {\n        'fileData': ('Academic_Pathway.pdf', pdf_bytes, 'application/pdf')\n    }\n    # For demo, just create a record with a link to the file\n    data = {\n        'Name': record.get('element_1', 'N/A'),\n        'Email__c': record.get('element_3', 'N/A'),\n        'Notes__c': 'Academic Pathway generated and sent.',\n    }\n    response = requests.post(\n        f\"{SALESFORCE_INSTANCE_URL}/services/data/v57.0/sobjects/{SALESFORCE_OBJECT}/\",\n        headers=headers,\n        data=json.dumps(data)\n    )\n    response.raise_for_status()\n    # For real PDF upload, use Salesforce ContentVersion API.\n\n# =============== TRACKING INTERFACE (FLASK) ===============\n\napp = Flask(__name__)\napp.secret_key = FLASK_SECRET_KEY\n\n# In-memory tracking for demo. ===========================\ndef update_master_sheet(students: List[Dict]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Update the Google Sheet master record with student data.\n    Overwrites rows 2+ with new data.\n    \"\"\"\n    service = build('sheets', 'v4', credentials=creds, cache_discovery=False)\n    sheet = service.spreadsheets()\n    # Get header row\n    result = sheet.values().get(spreadsheetId=GOOGLE_SHEETS_ID, range='A1:Z1').execute()\n    headers = result.get('values', [[]])[0]\n    values = []\n    for student in students:\n        row = [student.get(h, doc_copy['id']\n    # Replace placeholders\n    requests_list = [\n        {\n            'replaceAllText': {\n                'containsText': {'text': '{{name}}', 'matchCase': True},\n                'replaceText': student.get('name', '')\n            }\n        },\n        {\n            'replaceAllText': {\n                'containsText': {'text': '{{email}}', 'matchCase': True},\n ...}\n\n# ======================= MACHFORM INTEGRATION ===========================\ndef fetch_machform_data() -> List[Dict]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Fetches all entries from the 3 MachForms and merges by student email.\n    Returns a list of unique student records.\n    \"\"\"\n    all_entries = []\n    for endpoint, api_key in zip(MACHFORM_ENDPOINTS, MACHFORM_API_KEYS):\n        if not api_key:\n            continue\n        headers = {'Authorization': f'Bearer {api_key}'}\n        try:\n            resp = requests.get(endpoint, headers=headers, timeout=30)\n            resp.raise_for_status()\n            entries = resp.json().get('entries', [])\n            all_entries.append(entries)\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"Error fetching MachForm {endpoint}: {e}\")\n            continue\n    # Merge entries by student email\n    students = {}\n    for form_entries in all_entries:\n        for entry in form_entries:\n            # Normalize email key\n            email = entry.get('email') or entry.get('Email') or entry.get('student_email')\n            if not email:\n                continue\n            if email not in students:\n                students[email] = {}\n            students[email].update(entry)\n    return list(students.values())\n\n# ======================= GOOGLE SHEETS INTEGRATION ===========================\ndef update_master_sheet(students: List[Dict]):\n    \"\"\"\n    Update the Google Sheet master record with student data.\n    Overwrites all rows starting from row 2.\n    \"\"\"\n    service = build('sheets', 'v4', credentials=creds, cache_discovery=False)\n    sheet = service.spreadsheets()\n    # Get header row\n    result = sheet.values().get(spreadsheetId=GOOGLE_SHEETS_ID, range='A1:Z1').execute()\n    headers = result.get('values', [[]])[0]\n    values = []\n    for student in students:\n        row = [student.get(h, '') for h in headers]\n        values.append(row)\n    # Write starting from row 2\n    body = {'values': values}\n    sheet.values().update(\n        spreadsheetId=GOOGLE_SHEETS_ID,\n        range='A2',\n        valueInputOption='RAW',\n        body=body\n    ).execute()\n\n# ======================= OPENAI INTEGRATION ===========================\ndef generate_academic_pathway(student: Dict) -> str:\n    \"\"\"\n    Generate personalized academic pathway using OpenAI.\n    Returns the pathway text.\n    \"\"\"\n    client = OpenAI(api_key=OPENAI_API_KEY)\n    prompt = (\n        f\"Student Profile:\\n\"\n        f\"Name: {student.get('name') or student.get('Name')}\\n\"\n        f\"Email: {student.get('email')}\\n\"\n        f\"Academic Interests: {student.get('interests', '')}\\n\"\n        f\"Previous Education: {student.get('education', '')}\\n\"\n        f\"Goals: {student.get('goals', '')}\\n\"\n        f\"Other Info: {json.dumps(student)}\\n\\n\"\n        \"Based on the above, generate a personalized academic pathway (2 paragraphs).\"\n    )\n    response = client.chat.completions.create(\n        model=\"gpt-4\",\n        messages=[{\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": prompt}]\n    )\n    return response.choices[0].message.content.strip()\n\n# ======================= GOOGLE DOCS TEMPLATE FILLING ===========================\ndef fill_google_doc_template(student: Dict, pathway: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"\n    Fill Google Docs template and return document ID.\n    \"\"\"\n    docs_service = build('docs', 'v1', credentials=creds, cache_discovery=False)\n    drive_service = build('drive', 'v3', credentials=creds, cache_discovery=False)\n    # Copy template\n    body = {'name': f\"Academic Pathway - {student.get('name', student.get('email'))}\"}\n    doc_copy = drive_service.files().copy(\n        fileId=GOOGLE_DOCS_TEMPLATE_ID,\n        body=body\n    ).execute()\n    doc_id = doc_copy['id']\n    # Replace placeholders\n    requests_list = [\n        {\n            'replaceAllText': {\n                'containsText': {'text': '{{name}}', 'matchCase': True},\n                'replaceText': student.get('name', '')\n            }\n        },\n        {\n            'replaceAllText': {\n                'containsText': {'text': '{{email}}', 'matchCase': True},\n                'replaceText': student.get('email', '')\n            }\n        },\n        {\n            'replaceAllText': {\n                'containsText': {'text': '{{academic_pathway}}', 'matchCase': True},\n                'replaceText': pathway\n            }\n        }\n    ]\n ===========================\ndef export_doc_as_pdf(doc_id: str) -> bytes:\n    \"\"\"\n    Exports a Google Doc as PDF and returns the PDF bytes.\n    \"\"\"\n    drive_service = build('drive', 'v3', credentials=creds, cache_discovery=False)\n    request = drive_service.files().export_media(fileId=doc_id, mimeType='application/pdf')\n    fh = io.BytesIO()\n    downloader = MediaIoBaseDownload(fh, request)\n    done = False\n    while not done:\n        status, done = downloader.next_chunk()\n    fh.seek(0)\n    return fh.read()\n\n# ======================= EMAIL SENDING Disposition('attachment')\n    )\n    message.attachment = attachment\n    sg = SendGridAPIClient(SENDGRID_API_KEY)\n    sg.send(message)\n\n# ======================= SALESFORCE INTEGRATION
